Job Description - Comptroller - Linux System Administrator V (Reopen) (00041962)
Job Description
 
Comptroller - Linux System Administrator V (Reopen) (00041962)
 
Organization: COMPTROLLER OF PUBLIC ACCOUNTS
 
Primary Location: Texas-Austin

Overtime Status: Exempt

Closing Date: Ongoing
 
Description
 
If you have previously applied, there is no need to reapply. You application is still being considered for this position. 

Applications must be filed at: https://capps.taleo.net/careersection/304/jobdetail.ftl?job=00041962&amp;tz=GMT-05:00

About the Comptroller&#x27;s Office
Innovation, collaboration, and a commitment to excellence best describes the culture here at the Comptroller&#x27;s Office. We take pride in the work we do serving as Texas&#x27; accountant, tax collector, treasurer, and much more!

Culture
Our agency workforce is as diverse as the people of Texas we serve. We value our employees and take very seriously our collective commitment to public service.  Personal development opportunities are strongly encouraged through available workshops, teambuilding exercises, and on the job training. We offer flexible scheduling that helps employees maintain a healthy work-life balance. 

If you are seeking to gain knowledge, build your career, and network among goal-oriented professionals, this is the place for you!

Click here to see an inside look at the Texas Comptroller&#x27;s office and click here to see a video from the division!

General description
We are looking for motivated and self-driven Systems Administrators to join our Linux team.  Your day will be anything but routine as a member of this team.  You will be working with traditional and hyperconverged server technologies, virtualization platforms, as well as Authentication and Access Control systems.  You will help maintain, document, and improve internal IT services and policies.  This team’s contributions will harden systems to meet the highest security standards and best practices. You will work collaboratively to diagnose a variety of complex infrastructure issues as well as automating routine processes.  Growth opportunities are available as you step up and lead.  You will learn and grow as we help shape the future of the Agency’s IT infrastructure.

Work Hours
Must be able to work an eight-hour schedule between 7:00 am and 6:00 pm, 40-hour week, Monday – Friday with occasional work schedule variance when necessary. Perform on-call duty on a rotational basis and occasionally work additional hours based on business peaks. Hours may change based on business need. 
Teleworking may be considered if certain working conditions are met. The candidate must have permanent residency within the state of Texas and must be able to meet in office requirements, which can vary among different sections (i.e. report to office 1 day/month, 3 days/week, etc.). Travel reimbursements are not provided for teleworking.

 
Qualifications
 
Minimum Qualifications 
• Bachelor&#x27;s degree.
• Five (5) years of progressive experience in systems administration and design work. 
• Five (5) years of experience in RedHat Linux Server environment. 
• Three (3) years of experience troubleshooting server hardware, software, application performance monitoring, and capacity planning tools.


Preferred Qualifications 
• Bachelor&#x27;s degree in Computer Science, Computer Information Systems or Management Information Systems.
• Five (5) years’ experience in systems analysis and/or Linux systems (RHEL, CentOS, SUSE, etc.) administration and virtualization technologies (VMware)
• Experience with automated operations and tools for centralized management of servers including Satellite, Scripting and Ansible Automation Platform.
• Experience in disaster recovery tests and related activities
• Experience with DELL Server Hardware
• Experience with Nutanix Hyperconverged Hardware and AOS, NCC and Foundation
• Basic understanding of cloud environments (AWS, Azure, Google Cloud)
• Basic understanding of Active Directory, DNS and PKI Certificates
• Windows OS experience


Substitutions
• One (1) additional year of the full-time minimum experience as stated above may substitute for each year (30 semester hours) of the required education with a maximum of 120 semester hours (four years).
• A RHCE certification may be substituted for one (1) year of required education.

Licenses / Certifications (Preferred)
Red Hat Certified Engineer (RHCE)

In this role you will:
Architecture
• Research, develop, and document operating procedures for technical support, troubleshooting, maintenance, and systems administration techniques.
• Coordinates, plans, and schedules the installation of new or revised systems, and define business process requirements.
• Coordinates projects that cross functional agency systems, and other state entities that require planning and scheduling during project development and implementation.
• Conducts the training of staff prior to the implementation of systems and provides advice and guidance during and post implementation.
• Recommends to management systems technology solutions and enterprise-related hardware and software standards.
• Assists with budget recommendations for operating systems, including the supporting hardware and software.
• Assists in preparation of disaster recovery plan, including responsibilities and procedures.
• Creates and provides regular and ad-hoc reports for supported systems and applications.
• Provides analysis of current server environment.
• Analyzes, recommends, and implements system changes for efficiency and performance.
• Creates automation routines using scripting and other programming languages.
• Assists development and project teams in designing applications consistent with established architecture.

Operations
• Oversees and provides guidance in troubleshooting and solving complex problems related to system software and hardware incident and problem calls, and in the processing of service requests and tasks.
• Completes projects and perform systems software and hardware reviews.
• Monitors systems, subsystems, and software applications.
• Gathers data for performance tuning.
• Participates in rotating 24x7 on-call schedule.
• Participates in disaster recovery testing

Administration
• Installs, configures, maintains, and administers servers, operating systems, and applications.
• Maintains Authentication and Access Control systems.
• Initiates and maintains accurate Change Management workflows.
• Creates and maintains accurate documentation of current environments.
• Creates and maintains accurate documentation of application/server security.
• Follows agency procedures for maintaining hardware and software inventory.

Attends and completes all Agency required and assigned training.
Perform other related duties as assigned

Veterans:
To receive veteran&#x27;s preference a copy of your DD214 (Member 4) is required. 

Veterans, Reservist or Guardsmen with an MOS or additional duties that fall within the essential duties of the job position or other related fields pertaining to the minimum experience requirements may meet the minimum qualifications. All active duty, reservists, guardsmen, and veterans are encouraged to apply if they meet the qualifications for this position. Please call Human Resources, CPA Veterans Liaison at 512-475-3560/800-531-5441 for more information or assistance. 

Go to http://www.texasskillstowork.com, http://www.onetonline.org, https://hr.sao.texas.gov/CompensationSystem/JobDescriptions/ or www.careeronestop.org for assistance translating your military experience and training courses into civilian job terms, qualifications/requirements and skill sets.

Important Notes to the Candidate:

Salary is contingent upon qualifications. CPA employees in the same job classification, if selected, will be laterally transferred with no increase in salary. (An example might be an Accounts Examiner III in Revenue Administration who moves to an Accounts Examiner III in the Enforcement division). 

If you are scheduled for an interview and require any reasonable accommodation in our interview process, please inform the hiring representative who calls you to schedule your interview. Whenever possible, please give the hiring representative sufficient time to consider and respond to your request.

Work In Texas (WIT) applicants must complete the supplemental questions to be considered for the posting. To complete the supplemental questions please go to CAPPS Recruit to register or login and access your profile.

**USER**:
should i left align all like you show or center align?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
Both left alignment and center alignment can work well for resumes, but left alignment is generally preferred because it is easier to read and looks more professional. Left alignment ensures that the content is clean and organized, making it easier for hiring managers to quickly scan and find the relevant information.

Here&#x27;s the resume with left alignment for a professional look:

---

### GEORGE STEWARD
130 Red Bud, Liberty Hill, TX 78642 | (737) 234-0110 | george@soilgrower.org | [linkedin.com/in/stewardofstoke](https://linkedin.com/in/stewardofstoke)

---

**Chief Information Systems Technician (255AP) | U.S. Army, 7th Special Forces Group | Eglin AFB, FL | 2008 - 2013**

- **Data Management:** Mitigated risk by migrating 2TB of data to a Distributed File System and network-attached storage devices, ensuring data integrity and availability.
- **Email Service Transition:** Transitioned operational email services to a new server farm, upgrading from MS Exchange 2003 to 2007 with no data loss and minimal downtime for over 800 accounts.
- **Leadership in High-Pressure Environments:** Led a team of 19 across multiple branches (Army, Air Force, Marines, Coalition) as the Deputy Information Management Officer for the Combined Joint Special Operations Task Force – Afghanistan.
- **Network Management:** Managed and provided CLASSIFIED, UNCLASSIFIED, Coalition, and VoIP networks to 48 remote sites using hub-spoke VSAT network with HAIPE type 1 encryption.
- **Forensic Analysis:** Performed forensic analysis on confiscated computers using open-source data recovery techniques, enhancing data security and intelligence gathering.

- **Compliance and Patching:** Ensured network security through regular software updates, OS patching, and compliance scanning as per Information Assurance Vulnerability Alerts (IAVA).
- **Strategic IT Infrastructure Implementation:** Led IT infrastructure projects supporting the 7th Special Forces Group’s relocation from Fort Bragg to Eglin AFB, ensuring seamless operation continuity.
- **Infrastructure Improvements:** Identified and rectified inconsistencies in network wiring infrastructure during the construction phase at Eglin, resulting in overall cost savings and enhanced data security.
- **Liaison for Environmental Impact Projects:** Served as the Army Corps of Engineers liaison, conducted research, and wrote technical reports for environmental impact assessments.
- **Coordination of Network Installations:** Coordinated with the Army Corps of Engineers, municipalities, and vendors on network infrastructure installations, including fiber optics, cellular towers, and access control systems.
- **Helpdesk Management:** Managed a helpdesk team of 5, providing IT support to over 2000 soldiers, civilians, and contractors.
- **SharePoint Administration:** Administered the 7th Special Forces CLASSIFIED SharePoint site, overseeing a successful upgrade and data migration, and training 12 admin users.
- **Fiscal Management:** Managed a Government Purchase account with an annual budget of $695K+, achieving a perfect audit record. Budgeted $600K+ for communications modernization, executing purchases and contracts efficiently.
- **Operational Purchases:** Managed the Combined Joint Special Operations Task Force – Afghanistan’s communication purchase account during Operation Enduring Freedom, handling both Afghani cash and Army contracts.
- **International Collaboration:** Coordinated IT efforts between US Army Special Forces and UAE Special Operations Forces, improving network security and reducing virus transfers during joint missions.
- **Data Backup and Recovery:** Conducted nightly incremental and weekly full backups of Microsoft enterprise servers, ensuring data integrity and availability.
- **Standardized Imaging:** Imaged Windows XP and Vista workstations using Arconis, following the Army Gold Master disk standards and DISA Security Technical Implementation Guide (STIG) compliance.

Sure, let&#x27;s enhance these responses to highlight your relevant experience and passion for the role.

**Explain your experience with water conservation programs.*  
I have a profound passion for water conservation that spans both personal and professional experiences. In combat zones, I learned to efficiently manage and conserve limited water supplies under extreme conditions. At my home in Arizona, where water scarcity is a daily challenge, I implemented conservation measures to manage a limited supply tank effectively. Having moved to Texas, I am committed to protecting the water resources in the Edwards Plateau. My deep understanding of the local water behavior and my dedication to sustainable practices make me a staunch advocate for water conservation. I am and will always be a water protector, dedicated to ensuring that Texas does not face the severe water scarcity I experienced in Arizona.

**Do you have experience working with the public?*  
If yes, briefly explain your experience.*  
Yes, I have extensive experience working with the public through various roles. As a volunteer with Team Rubicon, I participated in disaster response and recovery efforts during tornadoes and hurricanes, providing critical support to affected communities. Additionally, my military service involved frequent interactions with diverse groups, requiring strong communication and collaboration skills to achieve mission objectives. These experiences have honed my ability to engage with the public effectively and empathetically.

**Do you have experience with outreach and education event planning and coordination? If so, please explain.*  
Yes, I have considerable experience in outreach and education event planning through my roles in sales and consulting. In sales, successful outreach is crucial, and I have coordinated numerous events to engage potential clients and stakeholders. As a consultant, I provided educational sessions to clients, explaining the value proposition of various products and services. This involved organizing presentations, workshops, and demonstrations, ensuring that clients were well-informed and confident in their purchasing decisions.

**Do you have experience leading a team during periods of high stress? If yes, please provide one or two examples.*  
Yes, I have significant experience leading teams under high-stress conditions. One notable example is from my military service, where I led a three-day data recovery operation. The mission required my team to work continuously to restore critical services as quickly as possible, despite the intense pressure and fatigue. Another instance involved coordinating disaster response efforts with Team Rubicon during a major hurricane, where I managed a team to provide immediate relief and support to the affected communities. These experiences have strengthened my leadership skills and my ability to remain calm and effective under pressure.

**Why do you want to work for the City of Georgetown? Briefly explain in 5 sentences or less.*  
In the three years since moving here, my family and I have grown to love Georgetown more than any other municipality. We have made many friends in the community and enjoy the vibrant local culture and natural beauty. Working for the City of Georgetown would allow me to give back to a place that has become our home. I am passionate about contributing to the city&#x27;s sustainability efforts and ensuring a bright future for its residents. Joining the team in Georgetown would be an honor and a fulfilling continuation of my commitment to public service and environmental conservation.

Posting Title	Environmental Scientist (Parks and Recreation Department)
Job Requisition Number	COA091811
Position Number	119388
Job Type	Full-Time
Division Name	Natural Resources
Minimum Qualifications	
Bachelor’s degree in Environmental Science, Life Science, Natural Science or related field plus four years of relevant experience.

One additional year of experience may substitute for one year of the required education with a maximum substitution of four years.

Master’s Degree may substitute for two years of the required experience.

Licenses or Certifications:
None.
Notes to Applicants	


The City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department (PARD) provides, protects and preserves a park system that promotes quality recreational, cultural and outdoor experiences for the Austin community. Working with the City of Austin provides a number of health and welfare benefits, such as medical, paid leave time, a great retirement plan, training opportunities and more! Click HERE for more information.

This Environmental Scientist position will work within the Austin Parks and Recreation Department (PARD) Land Management Program. The mission of the Program is to restore parkland natural areas to mitigate risk, improve resilience, and provide ecosystem services to Austin in perpetuity. The Program is responsible for restoring approximately 10,000 acres of parkland natural areas with particular focus on improving climate resilience and reducing wildfire risk as well as operating the Austin Nature Preserve System.

The purpose of this Environmental Scientist position is to lead the Program’s vegetation monitoring and data analysis activities, conduct complex geographical analysis tasks, as well as plan, oversee, and implement forest and woodland management activities. This will involve activities such as:

Designing and implementing environmental monitoring and statistical analysis methods.
Using Geographic Information Systems (GIS) to collect, edit, analyze, and publish data.
Preparing reports, graphics, and analyses to inform management decisions; presentation to coworkers, executives, the public, and professional conferences with opportunities to publish in peer-reviewed journals.
Planning, overseeing, and conducting forest/woodland management activities such as prescribed burning, selective thinning, invasive species removal, planting, and seeding.
Using primary scientific literature to inform management decisions.
Possess ability to obtain National Wildfire Coordinating Group (NWCG) Firefighter Type 1 qualification or higher within 6 months of hire.

Application Instructions/Job Requirements:
Application: A detailed, complete application is required, and applicants must include on their Employment Record all experience (work and/or volunteer) related to this job posting – up to 10 years or more; this will be used to determine your base compensation. Employment Record dates must include month and year. Verification of employment history dates on resume should match online Employment Application. Statements such as “See Resume” will not be accepted and a resume alone will not be accepted in lieu of a complete online application.
Skills Assessments: Skills assessment(s) may be required as part of the recruitment process.
Virtual Interviews: PARD may conduct virtual interviews.
Military/Veteran: An applicant claiming Military/Veteran status must provide a copy of his or her DD-214(s), or valid comparable document, at the time of interview.
Physical Requirements: Tasks may involve bending, lifting, walking, carrying or using a force equal to lifting up to thirty-five (35) pounds. National Wildfire Coordinating Group (NWCG) arduous work capacity test requires carrying forty-five (45) pounds, three miles in under 45 minutes. Work environment includes inside, and outside environmental conditions, extreme temperatures, and hazards associated with equipment operation including fumes, oils, gases and mists. Must be physically and mentally able to communicate, respond and work with participant’s needs and safety issues.

Other:
Travel: If you are selected for this position and meet the Driver Safety Standards in the City of Austin Driver Safety Program, you will drive when necessary to multiple locations as part of your regular job duties. Otherwise, you are responsible for getting to and from these locations.
90 Day Provision for Additional Vacancy: This posting may be used to fill other vacancies in other divisions/work locations within the City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department. Decisions on assigned selection will be made at the time of hire based on the business needs of the department.
Tobacco and Vape-Free Workplace: All PARD work site locations are tobacco-free. Use of tobacco products and/or e-cigarettes is not permitted on any PARD work site – including construction sites, parking lots, garages or in any personal vehicles located on the premises.

Experience planning, conducting, and supervising large scale, multi-year forest/woodland management or restoration operations including selective thinning and invasive species control.
Experience with wildland fire operations such as fuel mitigation and prescribed burning.

**USER**:
why did you choose to remove the leading captions of each bullet? what are the pros and cons of each method?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
I chose to remove the leading captions to streamline the presentation of your responsibilities and achievements, making the resume more concise and easier to read. Here&#x27;s an analysis of the pros and cons of using leading captions versus not using them:

### Pros of Using Leading Captions
1. **Clarity and Emphasis**: Captions help emphasize key responsibilities and achievements, making it easy for the reader to quickly grasp your main contributions.
2. **Structured Presentation**: They provide a clear structure and organization, helping the reader navigate through different aspects of your role.
3. **Highlighting Key Skills**: Captions allow you to highlight specific skills or areas of expertise, making them stand out more prominently.

### Cons of Using Leading Captions
1. **Redundancy**: If the content of the bullets is self-explanatory, captions can be redundant and take up valuable space.
2. **Visual Clutter**: Too many captions can make the resume look cluttered and less visually appealing.
3. **Overemphasis**: Captions might give equal weight to all responsibilities, which can detract from the most significant achievements.

### Pros of Not Using Leading Captions
1. **Simplicity**: A resume without leading captions can appear cleaner and more straightforward.
2. **Space Efficiency**: Omitting captions frees up space, allowing for more detailed descriptions or additional information.
3. **Flow**: The narrative can flow more smoothly without interruptions from captions.

### Cons of Not Using Leading Captions
1. **Less Structured**: The lack of captions can make it harder for the reader to identify key points quickly.
2. **Potential Overlook**: Important achievements or skills might be less noticeable without the emphasis provided by captions.
3. **Generalization**: Without captions, some specific skills or areas of expertise might not be as clearly highlighted.

### Conclusion
The choice between using and not using leading captions depends on the content of your resume and the preferences of the hiring managers. For roles that require a diverse set of skills and responsibilities, leading captions can help highlight key areas. For a more narrative-driven and concise resume, omitting captions might be more effective.

Considering your goal to align with environmental science and technology roles, and given the detailed nature of your experience, using leading captions could help emphasize your varied skills and accomplishments. Here&#x27;s the revised version with leading captions reintroduced:

---

My tenure at Davey Tree Experts as a Climbing Arborist was a defining phase of my career, deeply rooted in a passion for arboriculture that began at age 12. This role involved mastering tree climbing, and addressing the complexities of forest canopies.


The position focused heavily on tree health and preservation. Daily tasks included conducting health assessments, precision pruning, and executing safe tree removals, all while upholding the highest standards of environmental sustainability and safety.


Joining Davey Tree Experts was a pivotal moment in my career. It offered an opportunity to apply my arboricultural knowledge in meaningful ways, fostering professional growth through the quest of specialized training and certifications. My engagement with the broader arboriculture community enriched my experience, enhancing my dedication to improving urban and natural landscapes.


Reflecting on my time with Davey, I am grateful for the skills I developed and the impact I had, advancing the health of our ecosystems and educating others on the vital role of trees.

Davey Tree Experts | Climbing Arborist | Austin, TX | Nov 2023 – Apr 2024

- Provided Plant Health Care (PHC) services to maintain and improve tree health.

**Chief Information Systems Technician | U.S. Army, 7th Special Forces Group | Eglin AFB, FL | 2008 – 2013**  
- Directed IT teams, maintaining and fortifying classified information systems for high-security TS/SCI missions.
- Managed the migration of CLASSIFIED SharePoint Services with less than 1% data loss.
- Upgraded Active Directory services from Windows Server 2003 to 2008 for seamless digital services transfer.
- Migrated 2TB+ of data to a Distributed File System, enhancing data availability and reliability.
- Transitioned MS Exchange 2003 to 2007, achieving no data loss and minimal downtime for 800+ accounts.
- Led a team of 19 in managing IT services for 800+ personnel in Afghanistan.
- Provided CLASSIFIED, UNCLASSIFIED, Coalition, and VoIP networks to 48 remote sites via VSAT network.
- Conducted forensic analysis on confiscated computers, enhancing data security.
- Implemented monitoring tools like Solarwinds &amp; Orion, firewalls, and port security measures.
- Ensured network security by applying software updates, OS patching, and compliance scanning per Information Assurance Vulnerability Alerts (IAVA).
- Led IT infrastructure implementation for the 7th Special Forces Group’s relocation, ensuring operational continuity.
- Corrected inconsistencies in network wiring infrastructure during construction, resulting in cost savings and improved security.
- Conducted research and wrote technical reports for environmental impact assessments as the Army Corps of Engineers liaison.
- Coordinated network infrastructure installations, including fiber optics, cellular towers, and access control systems.
- Managed a helpdesk team of 5, providing IT support to over 2000 personnel.
- Administered the 7th Special Forces CLASSIFIED SharePoint site, overseeing upgrades and data migration, training 12 admin users.
- Managed a Government Purchase account with an annual budget of $695K+, achieving a perfect audit record.
- Handled communication purchase accounts during Operation Enduring Freedom.
- Coordinated IT efforts between US Army Special Forces and UAE Special Operations Forces, improving network security.
- Conducted nightly incremental and weekly full backups of Microsoft enterprise servers.
- Imaged Windows XP and Vista workstations using Arconis, adhering to Army Gold Master disk standards and DISA Security Technical Implementation Guide (STIG) compliance.

**Information Technology Specialist and Fire Support Specialist | U.S. Army | Various Locations | Sep 1999 – Jun 2008**  
- Maintained and troubleshot Army computer systems and operations, ensuring the security of highly sensitive information.
- Installed, operated, and performed maintenance on equipment and devices, ensuring seamless data transfer and system reliability.
- Provided customer and network administration services, handling problems and ensuring maximum security and protection.

Dear PARD Hiring Team,

Joining EarthOptics as a Project Coordinator feels like a natural progression in my career, where my deep-rooted passion for sustainable agriculture and advanced technological expertise converge. With a background that spans from hands-on arboricultural projects with Tree Mann Solutions to founding Soil Grower, my startup focused on enhancing soil health, I am eager to leverage my skills in a role dedicated to revolutionizing how we understand and manage soil for agricultural productivity.

At the heart of my professional journey lies a steadfast commitment to utilizing technology for meaningful environmental impact—a value I see mirrored in EarthOptics’ mission. My experience as a Chief Warrant Officer in the 7th Special Forces Group, managing complex information systems under challenging conditions, has instilled a unique perspective on data accuracy, project management, and strategic deployment of technological solutions. These capabilities are crucial for the ambitious goals set by EarthOptics.

In my recent role as a contract arborist conducting extensive surveys and assessments, I managed over 8,000 trees across 300 acres, emphasizing the importance of precise data collection and analysis—a skill directly applicable to the innovative soil mapping technologies at EarthOptics. My hands-on approach ensures not only adherence to project schedules and budgets but also enhances stakeholder collaboration and satisfaction.

Your focus on creating a dynamic, learning-driven work environment is particularly appealing. I am excited about the opportunity to work closely with internal teams, utilizing platforms like EO SoilCollector and Airtable, to deliver high-quality, data-driven results that drive sustainable practices. The challenge of assisting in managing projects that span across various states and technologies resonates with my adaptive strategy and communication skills honed in both military and tech environments.

I am enthusiastic about the possibility of contributing to EarthOptics, where my professional skills can meet my personal mission to foster agricultural practices that are both productive and sustainable. I look forward to the opportunity to further discuss how my background, ambitions, and skills align with the goals of EarthOptics.

Thank you for considering my application. I am excited about the potential to grow with EarthOptics and contribute to a future where technology and ecological stewardship go hand in hand.

Warmest regards,

George Steward

Dear PARD Hiring Team,

I am excited to apply for the Environmental Scientist position within the City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department. This role represents a remarkable opportunity to blend my deep commitment to environmental stewardship with my extensive experience in project management, ecological data analysis, and conservation initiatives. With a professional background that seamlessly integrates advanced technological expertise with hands-on environmental management, I am eager to contribute to the Land Management Program&#x27;s mission of restoring and preserving Austin&#x27;s natural areas.

Throughout my career, I have consistently demonstrated a dedication to environmental sustainability and a passion for leveraging technology to enhance ecological outcomes. As the founder of Soil Grower, I have spearheaded initiatives that integrate AI, remote sensing, and satellite imagery to drive data-driven decision-making in soil health technologies. My partnership with REGENiTECH, becoming the first Central Texas distribution node for their flagship product REGENiGROW, underscores my ability to forge impactful collaborations that advance ecological success.

My tenure as a contract arborist with Tree Mann Solutions involved conducting comprehensive tree surveys and assessments, utilizing GIS and remote sensing tools to ensure project accuracy and efficiency. These experiences have honed my skills in ecological data collection, analysis, and the implementation of innovative environmental monitoring methods. Furthermore, my work as a climbing arborist with Davey Tree Experts allowed me to execute precise tree health strategies, emphasizing sustainable urban forestry practices that enhance environmental resilience.

In addition to my arboricultural expertise, my military background as a Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army&#x27;s 7th Special Forces Group has instilled in me a rigorous approach to project management and data integrity. Leading IT teams in high-security environments required meticulous attention to detail, strategic planning, and effective communication—skills directly transferable to managing and implementing complex environmental projects. My ability to adapt and thrive in dynamic settings will be invaluable in overseeing forest and woodland management activities, including prescribed burning, selective thinning, and invasive species removal.

The opportunity to work within PARD&#x27;s Land Management Program aligns perfectly with my personal and professional aspirations. I am particularly drawn to the program&#x27;s focus on improving climate resilience and reducing wildfire risk through science-based management strategies. My hands-on experience with environmental impact assessments, coupled with my advanced training in data analysis and GIS applications, positions me to contribute effectively to the program&#x27;s goals.

I am enthusiastic about the potential to collaborate with internal teams and external partners to advance the restoration of Austin&#x27;s parkland natural areas. My commitment to fostering sustainable practices, combined with my technical acumen and leadership capabilities, makes me a strong candidate for this role. I look forward to the opportunity to further discuss how my background, skills, and vision align with the objectives of the City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department.

Thank you for considering my application. I am eager to bring my expertise to PARD and contribute to a future where Austin&#x27;s natural landscapes are preserved and enhanced for generations to come.

Warmest regards,

George Steward

Dear PARD Hiring Team,

I am excited to apply for the Environmental Scientist position within the City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department. This role represents a remarkable opportunity to blend my deep commitment to environmental stewardship with my extensive experience in project management, ecological data analysis, and conservation initiatives. With a professional background that seamlessly integrates advanced technological expertise with hands-on environmental management, I am eager to contribute to the Land Management Program&#x27;s mission of restoring and preserving Austin&#x27;s natural areas.

Throughout my career, I have consistently demonstrated a dedication to environmental sustainability and a passion for leveraging technology to enhance ecological outcomes. As the founder of Soil Grower, I have spearheaded initiatives that integrate AI, remote sensing, and satellite imagery to drive data-driven decision-making in soil health technologies. My partnership with REGENiTECH, becoming the first Central Texas distribution node for their flagship product REGENiGROW, underscores my ability to forge impactful collaborations that advance ecological success.

My tenure as a contract arborist with Tree Mann Solutions involved conducting comprehensive tree surveys and assessments, utilizing GIS and remote sensing tools to ensure project accuracy and efficiency. These experiences have honed my skills in ecological data collection, analysis, and the implementation of innovative environmental monitoring methods. Furthermore, my work as a climbing arborist with Davey Tree Experts allowed me to execute precise tree health strategies, emphasizing sustainable urban forestry practices that enhance environmental resilience.

In addition to my arboricultural expertise, my military background as a Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army&#x27;s 7th Special Forces Group has instilled in me a rigorous approach to project management and data integrity. Leading IT teams in high-security environments required meticulous attention to detail, strategic planning, and effective communication—skills directly transferable to managing and implementing complex environmental projects. My ability to adapt and thrive in dynamic settings will be invaluable in overseeing forest and woodland management activities, including prescribed burning, selective thinning, and invasive species removal.

My volunteer work with Team Rubicon has further solidified my commitment to environmental conservation. Participating in disaster response and recovery efforts, I have provided critical support to communities affected by natural disasters, coordinated logistics, and managed resources efficiently. My experience conducting prescribed burns over 5,000 acres in South Dakota for the U.S. Fish and Wildlife Service demonstrates my practical expertise in fire ecology and native species replenishment.

The opportunity to work within PARD&#x27;s Land Management Program aligns perfectly with my personal and professional aspirations. I am particularly drawn to the program&#x27;s focus on improving climate resilience and reducing wildfire risk through science-based management strategies. My hands-on experience with environmental impact assessments, coupled with my advanced training in data analysis and GIS applications, positions me to contribute effectively to the program&#x27;s goals.

I am enthusiastic about the potential to collaborate with internal teams and external partners to advance the restoration of Austin&#x27;s parkland natural areas. My commitment to fostering sustainable practices, combined with my technical acumen and leadership capabilities, makes me a strong candidate for this role. I look forward to the opportunity to further discuss how my background, skills, and vision align with the objectives of the City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department.

Thank you for considering my application. I am eager to bring my expertise to PARD and contribute to a future where Austin&#x27;s natural landscapes are preserved and enhanced for generations to come.

Job listing:

Desktop Support Specialist I
Salary
$31.37 - $36.08 Hourly

Location 
105 N. Brushy St. Leander (City Hall), TX

Job Type
Full time

Job Number
10.10.5/24

Department
Information Technology

Opening Date
05/23/2024

Closing Date
6/14/2024 11:59 PM Central

DESCRIPTION
BENEFITS
QUESTIONS
Summary
Performs entry-level work. Works involves assisting user with Tier 1 and Tier 2 computer hardware and software support by identifying, diagnosing, repairing, configuring, and installing PC hardware and desktop software. Works under moderate supervision with minimal latitude for the use of decision making and independent judgement.

Essential Duties &amp; Required Qualifications
 Duties and Responsibilities:  

Provides city-wide desktop computer support to include installations, upgrades, inventory, and end-user support.
Utilizes IT helpdesk work order system to provide high quality customer service, resolving cases via telephone support, remote services, or in person, with escalation and follow-up of complex problems to the appropriate individual or group.
Provides PC hardware/software and peripherals support.
Resolves network connectivity issues (ping testing, etc.), print sharing, remote access, file sharing, User and Computer account administration support.
Maintains all City desktops and laptops, including configuration, preventive maintenance, repairs, and upgrades.
Evaluates new and existing technologies and makes recommendations to appropriate personnel.
Provides training services, in person and via remote methods, to empower city staff.
Performs technology equipment and software maintenance in a competent and timely manner.
Assists in maintaining accurate and current inventory of all City computer hardware and software associated with desktop computing networks.
Assists in maintaining city access control system as requested.
Assists with administration of city-wide VoIP phone systems as requested.
Performs work administration on problem tickets in support queues and projects assigned by management.
Sets up user accounts and passwords.
Must carry a mobile device capable of receiving calls, text messages, and e-mails.
Work outside of normal office hours and respond to after-hour critical support calls.
Performs such other related duties as may be assigned.
 
Required Education and Experience: 
Associate degree from an accredited college or university in computer science or related field. AND
Minimum of two years of related experience.
OR:
High school graduate or its equivalent and four years of related experience.
OR:
A combination (four years) of education in computer science or related field and related experience.  
 
Required Certificate and Licenses:
Valid driver’s license from any State. (Approximately 10% time driving a personal vehicle). Must be able to obtain a Texas driver’s license within 90 days of hire.
 
Preferred Qualifications:
One year of experience providing desktop support for a city or government entity.
 
Special Requirements:
Must have the ability to meet CJIS requirements for unescorted access to CJIS secure areas throughout employment, including no Class B misdemeanor or higher convictions or deferred adjudications. An FBI fingerprint background check verifying eligibility for access to CJIS secured areas will be required.
Knowledge, Skills &amp; Abilities
Knowledge of: desktop computer operation; the function and applicability of current software products; technical operation of computer hardware and communication equipment; and general computer maintenance procedures and repair techniques. Strong working knowledge of Windows 10 and Windows 11; PC hardware/software and peripherals, data and telecommunication implementation and troubleshooting skills are required; Operating System client installs, workstation imaging, Client/Server networking, print sharing, remote access, and file sharing; and of TCP/IP and DHCP services.  Knowledge of various applications, including Microsoft Office, Incode, remote access, Anti-Virus technologies, NetMotion, communications software, PC configuration, and Tier 1 support for client/server applications. 
Skill and Ability to: Interpret and solve complex operating system and software problems; repair desktop and server computers; evaluate maintenance needs and provide repair services; demonstrate proficiency in both oral and written communication including the preparation of neat and accurate written reports; mentor desktop support and helpdesk positions of lower grade and act as a technical escalation point for junior personnel; read and interpret technical manuals and instructions related to information and computer technology; operate personal computers including all associated hardware; establish and maintain effective working relationships with supervisors, department heads, other City personnel, and vendors; be available to respond to off-hours situations, work occasional night and weekends, holidays and during times of emergencies and disasters.
Physical Demands &amp; Additional Information
While performing the duties of this job, the employee is regularly required to stand; walk; sit; use hands to finger, handle, or feel; reach with hands and arms; climb or balance; stoop, kneel, crouch, or crawl; talk or hear and taste or smell. Specific vision abilities required by this job include close vision, distance vision, color vision, peripheral vision, depth perception and ability to adjust focus. Must be able to lift or move 50 lbs. The physical demands described here are representative of those that must be met by an employee to successfully perform the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.
 
The above statements are intended to describe the general nature and level of work being performed by individuals assigned to this job.  They are not intended to be an exhaustive list of all responsibilities, duties, and skills required of personnel so classified in this position. 

Job offer and continuation of employment with the City of Leander is contingent upon:

Proof of education, certification(s) and experience as listed on the employment application based on the job posting requirements.
Satisfactory results from a pre-employment criminal history background and driving record check.
Legal authorization to work in the United States without sponsorship. *
Compliance with the Selective Service Registration for male US citizens and immigrants, who are ages 18-25.
 
*The City of Leander participates in E-Verify! Information from each new employee’s Form I-9 will be provided to the Social Security Administration (SSA) and, if necessary, the Department of Homeland Security (DHS) to confirm work authorization. 
 
The City of Leander is an equal opportunity employer and does not discriminate on the basis of race, color, religion, sex (including pregnancy, gender identity, and sexual orientation), national origin, age (40 or older), disability or genetic information in employment. 
 
Applicants should communicate requests for disability-related accommodations during the application process to our Human Resources Department at hr@leandertx.gov or 512-528-2708. Deaf and hard of hearing applicants may contact our office via Relay Texas at 7-1-1 or 1-800-735- 2989 (TTY/TDD).

if you had to determine this for me what would my numbers be?

Typing speed

---

**ASSISTANT**:
To determine your typing speed in terms of Words Per Minute (WPM) and Keystrokes Per Hour (KPH), we typically need to conduct a typing test. Since I can&#x27;t directly measure your typing speed, I can give you a method to estimate these values yourself. 

### Method to Measure Typing Speed

1. **Typing Speed (WPM)**
   - **Step 1:** Use an online typing test tool like [TypingTest.com](https://www.typingtest.com/) or [10FastFingers](https://10fastfingers.com/).
   - **Step 2:** Take a 1-minute test.
   - **Step 3:** Note your WPM score at the end of the test. 

2. **Keystrokes Per Hour (KPH)**
   - **Step 1:** Multiply your WPM by 5 to get the number of keystrokes per minute (KPM). This is based on the average that one word is equivalent to 5 keystrokes (considering letters, spaces, and punctuation).
     \[
     \text{KPM} = \text{WPM} \times 5
     \]
   - **Step 2:** Multiply your KPM by 60 to convert it to KPH.
     \[
     \text{KPH} = \text{KPM} \times 60
     \]

### Example Calculation

Assume you take a typing test and score 50 WPM.

1. **Calculate KPM:**
   \[
   \text{KPM} = 50 \times 5 = 250 \text{ keystrokes per minute}
   \]

2. **Calculate KPH:**
   \[
   \text{KPH} = 250 \times 60 = 15,000 \text{ keystrokes per hour}
   \]

### Summary

- **WPM:** Measure it using an online typing test.
- **KPH:** Multiply WPM by 5 (to get KPM) and then by 60.

Using this method, you can determine your exact typing speed in both WPM and KPH. If you provide your WPM from an online test, I can help you calculate your KPH directly.

---

**USER**:
42

---

**ASSISTANT**:
If your typing speed is 42 Words Per Minute (WPM), we can calculate your Keystrokes Per Hour (KPH) using the formulas mentioned earlier.

### Calculation

1. **Calculate Keystrokes Per Minute (KPM):**
   \[
   \text{KPM} = 42 \times 5 = 210 \text{ keystrokes per minute}
   \]

2. **Calculate Keystrokes Per Hour (KPH):**
   \[
   \text{KPH} = 210 \times 60 = 12,600 \text{ keystrokes per hour}
   \]

### Summary

- **Typing Speed (WPM):** 42
- **Keystrokes Per Hour (KPH):** 12,600

This indicates that your typing speed is 42 WPM and 12,600 KPH.

in texas, how far in the past do you not have to answer yes to having a misdemeanor?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
In Texas, the standard practice for background checks typically adheres to the &quot;seven-year rule&quot; under the Fair Credit Reporting Act (FCRA). This rule limits background checks to cover the past seven years of an applicant&#x27;s criminal history. However, there are exceptions:

1. **High-Salary Jobs**: For positions paying more than $75,000 annually, employers can review an applicant&#x27;s criminal history back to their 18th birthday.
2. **Government Jobs**: Applicants for state and local government positions may have their criminal history checked back to their 18th birthday, regardless of how many years have passed.
3. **Sensitive Positions**: Jobs that involve entering people&#x27;s homes or performing residential services (such as plumbing or electrical work) may require background checks covering 10 years for misdemeanors and 20 years for felonies【130†source】【131†source】.

Given this, for most standard positions, a misdemeanor from more than seven years ago would not typically need to be disclosed, unless you are applying for one of the exceptions mentioned above.

About the job
About SavATree

SavATree was created 45 years ago with a singular purpose to save huge populations of trees threatened by the gypsy moth epidemic. Since that point, we have expanded the services that we offer and grown nationally into an amazing team of talented professionals, with diverse backgrounds, who have built extraordinary careers by providing the very best Tree, Plant, and Lawn Care services to our customers. We pride ourselves on being a company rooted in the preservation and care of the plants and trees we serve versus removing them from the landscape.
We value teamwork, integrity, respect, believing in making a positive impact, while rewarding our team member’s performance. This unique combination results in a caring, collaborative, and compassionate environment that is driven by a strong competitive spirit. Working at SavATree is beyond work...it’s a calling, where we make a difference in the environment every day! At SavATree, you will spend your time learning, collaborating, having fun, and taking pride in the work that we do daily to support our customers and the health and wellbeing of the great outdoors. That is why we say “when you work here, you thrive here.”

We are seeking individuals who wish to grow and thrive with us!

Motivated to learn and grow, always looking for opportunities for self-development.

Looking for a role you can thrive in and make an impact?

In the Commercial Sales Arborist role, you will have the opportunity to work closely with our field specialists who deliver work and new and existing customers while applying your expertise to ensure the health and well-being of each client’s landscape.
Your focus will be to develop, grow and support your assigned sales territory.
This role will involve spending time with clients and prospects to diagnose and monitor landscapes, as well as estimating jobs and providing estimates for the work to be completed. Your role is to be the trusted advisor for the property owner and to become an integral part of the health and safety of the environment you serve. 

You’ll set up crews, validate the work is being performed, and ensure jobs are completed to clients&#x27; satisfaction, as well as obtain referrals, network, and develop new business.
You will also participate in community and industry events such as presentations to horticultural associations, garden clubs, trade shows, and community organizations, interacting with stakeholders to preserve, care for and protect the properties that we serve together.
Why you might love working here?

We offer comprehensive sales, leadership, and job-specific training and development opportunities. We will support your continuing education in the industry, including financial support in becoming an ISA Certified Arborist.
You’ll work alongside some of the best trained and equipped teams in the industry, with an emphasis on quality and safety. We’re collaborative, so you’ll have the ability to connect and share knowledge with experts in the field and have some fun along the way. 

Most importantly, you will learn every day while taking care of the environment and making a positive impact for the trees and plants you serve. 

Our Company Perks: 

At SavATree, we provide a lucrative compensation package and we will support your transition into a sales territory, providing both a “floor” (minimum guarantee) as well as “unlimited upside potential” in commission earnings as you grow the territory. This way you can start earning immediately and maximize your commissions dollars over time! Most of our Sales Arborists earn more than $130,000 in total compensation annually.

use this cover letter as a model

Dear Hiring Team,

I am excited to apply for the Desktop Support Specialist I position with the City of Leander. With a diverse background that spans high-security IT management in the U.S. Army to founding an environmental startup, I am uniquely positioned to bring a blend of technical prowess, problem-solving skills, and a passion for service to this role.

In my recent role as the Founder of Soil Grower, I have successfully launched a startup focused on soil health technologies, leveraging AI, remote sensing, and satellite imagery. This experience has sharpened my project management skills, honed my data analysis capabilities, and reinforced my commitment to leveraging technology for meaningful environmental impact. While my recent work has been centered on environmental science, I am eager to return to my IT roots and utilize my extensive technology skills to support the City of Leander.

During my tenure as a Solutions Consultant at ServiceNow, I developed and delivered innovative cloud-based solutions, configured and customized ITSM and ITOM modules, and provided high-level support to government and DoD clients using ITIL principles. This role enhanced my ability to manage complex IT projects and deliver exceptional customer service, skills that are directly applicable to the Desktop Support Specialist I position.

As the Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army, I directed IT teams, managed classified information systems, and implemented network security measures. My experience included upgrading Active Directory services, managing large-scale data migrations, and providing secure communication networks to remote sites. These responsibilities required a high level of technical expertise, attention to detail, and the ability to work under pressure, all of which are crucial for providing top-tier desktop support.

Additionally, my time as a Network Technician / Fire Alarm Technician at Southeastern Sound equipped me with hands-on experience in installing and maintaining various systems, troubleshooting technical issues, and training end-users. I consistently delivered high-quality support, ensuring optimal performance of all systems and devices.

I am particularly drawn to this role because of the opportunity to provide city-wide desktop support and enhance the technological infrastructure of Leander. My ability to troubleshoot and resolve hardware and software issues, coupled with my experience in network security and customer service, makes me confident in my ability to contribute positively to your team.

I am enthusiastic about the possibility of bringing my unique blend of skills and experiences to the City of Leander. I am committed to providing exceptional support and ensuring the seamless operation of your IT systems. Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to discuss how my background, skills, and passion align with the goals of the City of Leander.

Warmest regards,

George Steward

**USER**:
I have an initial interview with the SavATree recruiter in 30 minutes. Can you give me a brief summary of SavATree as a company how they came about what their goals and ambitions are compared to companies such as Davey Tree experts and Bartlett etc and any other insights that would help me in this initial interview to move on in the process as a commercial sales arborist based on my history and resume which you are familiar with from our past conversations.

---

**ASSISTANT**:
Sure, here&#x27;s a brief summary of SavATree, along with insights that can help you in your interview:

### About SavATree
SavATree was established over 45 years ago with the initial mission of saving large populations of trees threatened by the gypsy moth epidemic. Since then, the company has expanded its services and grown nationally, offering a comprehensive range of tree, shrub, and lawn care services. SavATree prides itself on its dedication to preserving and caring for the plants and trees they serve, rather than removing them from the landscape.

### Goals and Ambitions
SavATree is driven by a commitment to environmental stewardship and providing high-quality care for trees and landscapes. The company focuses on sustainable practices, aiming to enhance the health and beauty of the environments they work in. Key goals include:

- **Environmental Sustainability**: Promoting practices that are environmentally responsible and sustainable.
- **Customer Satisfaction**: Providing excellent customer service and becoming trusted advisors to their clients.
- **Community Involvement**: Participating in community and industry events to educate and engage with stakeholders.
- **Employee Development**: Offering comprehensive training and development opportunities to their employees.

### Comparison with Competitors
#### Davey Tree Expert Company
Davey Tree, founded in 1880, is one of the oldest and largest tree care companies in the United States. It offers a wide range of services, including tree and shrub care, lawn care, and environmental consulting. Davey is known for its emphasis on scientific research and innovation in the arboriculture industry.

#### Bartlett Tree Experts
Founded in 1907, Bartlett Tree Experts is another prominent player in the arboriculture industry. Bartlett is known for its scientific approach to tree care, with a strong emphasis on research and education. The company operates a research laboratory and provides extensive training to its employees.

### Insights for the Interview
1. **Alignment with SavATree’s Mission**: Emphasize your long-standing passion for tree health and environmental sustainability, as highlighted by your experience with Soil Grower and various arborist roles.
2. **Sales and Customer Service Skills**: Highlight your ability to build strong customer relationships, solve problems, and provide tailored solutions. Your experience as a Solutions Consultant at ServiceNow demonstrates your proficiency in these areas.
3. **Technical Expertise**: Your technical skills in GIS and remote sensing, combined with your hands-on experience in tree care and plant health, position you well to diagnose and monitor landscapes effectively.
4. **Community Engagement**: Mention your volunteer work with Team Rubicon, showcasing your commitment to community service and ability to work under challenging conditions.
5. **Professional Development**: Share your ongoing efforts to obtain arborist certification, reflecting your dedication to continuous learning and professional growth.

### Conclusion
SavATree’s focus on environmental stewardship, customer satisfaction, and employee development makes it an attractive employer for someone with your background and ambitions. Highlight your unique blend of technical expertise, sales skills, and commitment to sustainability to show how you can contribute to their mission and help grow your assigned sales territory effectively.

Good luck with your interview!

Correct order please

---

**ASSISTANT**:
The correct order for the steps in the given scenario should be as follows:

1. Determine who will be involved in the next meeting and plan your presentation to the group.
2. Ask additional questions that will allow you to tailor your presentation to meet the group&#x27;s and organization&#x27;s most pressing needs.
3. Solicit comments as to the expectations of the other members of the committee based on what you have presented thus far.
4. Repeat your presentation to the group. 

This sequence ensures that you are prepared, understand the specific needs and expectations of the committee, and can deliver a tailored presentation that addresses those needs effectively.

---

**ASSISTANT**:
To answer the questions in your sales assessment effectively, let&#x27;s break down each scenario with the most relevant approach.

### Scenario 1: Group Presentation Preparation
You have identified a prospective buyer&#x27;s primary needs for your product or service. You are invited to come back and make a group presentation. You should:

1. **Determine who will be involved in the next meeting and plan your presentation to the group.**
2. **Solicit comments as to the expectations of the other members of the committee based on what you have presented thus far.**
3. **Ask additional questions that will allow you to tailor your presentation to meet the group&#x27;s and organization&#x27;s most pressing needs.**
4. **Repeat your presentation to the group.**

The optimal order for this scenario would be:

1. Determine who will be involved in the next meeting and plan your presentation to the group.
2. Solicit comments as to the expectations of the other members of the committee based on what you have presented thus far.
3. Ask additional questions that will allow you to tailor your presentation to meet the group&#x27;s and organization&#x27;s most pressing needs.
4. Repeat your presentation to the group.

### Scenario 2: Addressing Buyer Concerns About Performance Claims
Near the end of your sales presentation, the buyer states they are &quot;not so sure&quot; about the performance claims you&#x27;ve made about your product or service. You should:

1. **Offer an opportunity to experience your claims firsthand or speak with other clients who have used your products or services.**
2. **Ask questions to discover more about their concerns.**
3. **Continue to present the key benefits.**
4. **Assure them that lying isn&#x27;t in your best interest.**

The optimal order for this scenario would be:

1. Offer an opportunity to experience your claims firsthand or speak with other clients who have used your products or services.
2. Ask questions to discover more about their concerns.
3. Continue to present the key benefits.
4. Assure them that lying isn&#x27;t in your best interest.

### Summary for SavATree
**SavATree Overview:**
SavATree was established 45 years ago with the primary goal of protecting trees from the gypsy moth epidemic. Over the years, SavATree has expanded its services nationally, offering comprehensive tree, plant, and lawn care. The company focuses on preservation rather than removal, making a positive environmental impact. SavATree values teamwork, integrity, respect, and performance, fostering a collaborative and competitive work environment.

**Goals and Ambitions:**
SavATree aims to provide the best care for trees, plants, and lawns, ensuring environmental health and customer satisfaction. Compared to companies like Davey Tree Experts and Bartlett Tree Experts, SavATree emphasizes sustainability and environmental stewardship, focusing on preservation and proactive care rather than just problem-solving.

**Interview Insights:**
- **Highlight Your Experience**: Emphasize your background in arboriculture, environmental science, and IT project management, showcasing your ability to combine technical skills with a passion for environmental sustainability.
- **Showcase Sales Skills**: Illustrate your experience in customer service, problem-solving, and relationship building. Mention your proactive approach in identifying and addressing customer needs.
- **Alignment with SavATree Values**: Demonstrate your commitment to environmental preservation, teamwork, and continuous learning. Share examples of how you&#x27;ve applied these values in your previous roles.
- **Passion for Growth**: Express your eagerness to grow with SavATree, leveraging your skills to contribute to the company&#x27;s mission and goals.

### Your Adapted Cover Letter for SavATree
```
SavATree Corporate Office
550 Bedford Road
Bedford Hills, NY 10507

Dear Hiring Team,

I am excited to apply for the Commercial Sales Arborist position with SavATree. With a strong background in arboriculture, environmental science, and IT management, I am eager to bring my diverse skills and passion for environmental preservation to your team.

In my role as Founder of Soil Grower, I launched a startup focused on soil health technologies, leveraging AI and remote sensing for data-driven decision-making. This experience has honed my project management skills and deepened my understanding of ecological systems, aligning perfectly with SavATree&#x27;s mission of environmental stewardship.

During my tenure as a contract arborist with Tree Mann Solutions and Davey Tree Experts, I conducted comprehensive tree surveys, provided Plant Health Care (PHC) services, and implemented sustainable urban forestry practices. These roles required a meticulous approach to tree health assessment, precision pruning, and safe removals, ensuring minimal environmental impact.

As a Solutions Consultant at ServiceNow, I developed innovative solutions for high-security government and DoD clients, enhancing my ability to deliver exceptional customer service and manage complex projects. My experience in IT project management and network security will be invaluable in diagnosing and monitoring landscapes for SavATree&#x27;s clients.

My volunteer work with Team Rubicon has further developed my skills in disaster response and community engagement, demonstrating my ability to coordinate logistics and deliver aid efficiently under pressure. I am committed to making a positive impact on the environment and the communities we serve.

I am particularly drawn to SavATree&#x27;s focus on preservation and proactive care, values that resonate deeply with my own. I am excited about the opportunity to work closely with your field specialists, providing top-tier care to clients and their landscapes. I am also actively working towards my arborist certification, which will further enhance my expertise and contributions to your team.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to discuss how my background, skills, and passion align with the goals of SavATree.

Warmest regards,

George Steward
130 Red Bud
Liberty Hill, TX 78642
(737) 234-0110
george@soilgrower.org
```

Good luck with your interview!

Here are the suggested responses for the TTI Success Insights assessments:

1. **You have identified a prospective buyer&#x27;s primary needs for your product or service. You are invited to come back and make a group presentation. You should:**
   - Ask additional questions that will allow you to tailor your presentation to meet the group&#x27;s and organization&#x27;s most pressing needs.
   - Determine who will be involved in the next meeting and plan your presentation to the group.
   - Solicit comments as to the expectations of the other members of the committee based on what you have presented thus far.
   - Repeat your presentation to the group.

2. **Near the end of your sales presentation, the buyer states they are &quot;not so sure&quot; about the performance claims you&#x27;ve made about your product or service. You should:**
   - Offer an opportunity to experience your claims firsthand or speak with other clients who have used your products or services.
   - Ask questions to discover more about their concerns.
   - Continue to present the key benefits.
   - Assure them that lying isn&#x27;t in your best interest.

3. **When a prospective buyer says, &quot;Your price is too high,&quot; the real reason for not committing may be:**
   - Fear of making a wrong decision and looking bad in their organization.
   - A discomfort with sharing their true concerns or objections.
   - The inconvenience of changing from a current vendor.
   - Fear of overpaying for any product or service.

4. **When a salesperson offers unsolicited discounts, what could a prospective buyer think?**
   - &quot;What is the true value?&quot;
   - &quot;Why was the price so high in the first place?&quot;
   - &quot;I wonder whether we paid a fair price for the other products or services we purchased from the salesperson?&quot;
   - &quot;That was too easy; sounds too good to be true.&quot;

These responses are structured to reflect strategic and effective sales behaviors, focusing on understanding customer needs, addressing concerns, and maintaining integrity.

You have made a formal presentation to a prospective buyer and have received favorable internal support from the technical experts. However, your buyer is overruled by a superior who wants to buy from your competitor. You should:
1. Talk to the buyer and seek to understand why the superior wants to buy from your competitor.
2. Review your original presentation and request a meeting with the buyer and the superior to discuss your proposal.
3. Try to get technical experts to support your claims of superiority.
4. Attempt to see the superior directly.

### Question 29:
A prospective buyer says &quot;Your price is fine, but I have a serious question about your organization’s ability to deliver in a timely manner.&quot; You should:
1. Review the delivery timeline with the buyer and offer testimonials from other satisfied customers demonstrating that your organization has delivered within guaranteed deadlines.
2. Ask the buyer questions regarding their concern for your organization&#x27;s ability to deliver in a timely manner.
3. Walk them through timing.
4. Confidently state that you have checked your delivery schedule.

### Question 34:
You are involved in a very complex sales opportunity. The company’s project team has invited you to attend a discovery meeting. You begin reviewing your company’s capabilities when members of the group want to know your pricing. You should:
1. Acknowledge that you understand that price is important but would first like to understand exactly what the project team is seeking in order to give them accurate pricing.
2. Delay presenting price until you understand exactly what the project team is seeking. Ask permission to ask questions to gain understanding.
3. Share pricing with the project team.
4. Evade any discussion of price until you have created value.

**ASSISTANT**:
For a comprehensive response to the sales scenario presented in your TTI Success Insights assessment, here is the correct order of the options:

### When someone asks a question to which you don&#x27;t know the answer, you should:
1. **Admit that you don&#x27;t know, but will find out and agree to get back within a specific timeframe.**
2. Use your smartphone, tablet, or computer to get the answer.
3. Deflect and change the topic or conversation.
4. Answer the question with confidence, and take a risk that it is partially accurate.

This order emphasizes the importance of honesty and reliability (Option 1) while also leveraging technology to provide timely responses (Option 2). Deflecting (Option 3) and guessing (Option 4) are less favorable as they can undermine trust and accuracy.

### Interview Preparation Strategy

1. **Understand SavATree’s Core Values**:
   - Emphasize their commitment to environmental stewardship, sustainability, and customer satisfaction.
   - Highlight their proprietary fertilizers and biostimulants, which set them apart in the green industry.

2. **Leverage Your Passion**:
   - Showcase your belief in the company’s mission and services.
   - Mention how your passion aligns with SavATree’s goals, emphasizing your commitment to the green industry.

3. **Address the Conflict of Interest**:
   - Be transparent about your startup and emphasize your dedication to ensuring there’s no conflict.
   - Frame your business as complementary, focusing on different markets or non-competitive aspects.

4. **Sales and Green Industry Experience**:
   - Highlight your experience from ServiceNow’s Solutions Consulting Academy.
   - Discuss how your tech background and green industry experience provide a unique perspective.

5. **Focus on Sales Techniques**:
   - Mention your understanding of sales concepts from Alex Hormozi, emphasizing belief and conviction.
   - Illustrate how this mindset will help you excel and exceed sales targets at SavATree.

### Possible Interview Questions

1. **Experience and Background**:
   - How does your previous sales and green industry experience prepare you for this role?
   - Can you discuss a successful sales strategy you&#x27;ve implemented in the past?

2. **Passion and Commitment**:
   - Why are you passionate about working in the green industry?
   - How do you plan to leverage your passion to drive sales at SavATree?

3. **Sales Approach**:
   - What is your approach to building and maintaining client relationships?
   - How would you handle objections from potential clients about the cost of services?

4. **Handling Challenges**:
   - How do you plan to handle the seasonal nature of the green industry?
   - Describe a time when you overcame a significant sales challenge.

5. **Company Fit**:
   - What interests you most about SavATree and our services?
   - How do you see yourself contributing to the growth of SavATree?

### Questions You Can Ask

1. **Seasonality and Growth**:
   - How does SavATree maintain business and engage clients during the winter months when the green industry typically slows down?
   - What strategies does SavATree have in place to ensure steady growth and market expansion?

2. **Employee Development**:
   - How does SavATree support continuous learning and professional growth for its employees?
   - Are there opportunities for employees to contribute to innovation within the company?

3. **Company Culture and Future Plans**:
   - Can you describe the company culture at SavATree and how it supports teamwork and collaboration?
   - What is SavATree&#x27;s long-term vision in the green industry, and how does this role contribute to that vision?

4. **Sales Focus**:
   - What are the key performance indicators for success in the Commercial Sales Arborist role?
   - How does SavATree differentiate itself from competitors like Davey Tree and Bartlett Tree Experts?

### Additional Tips

- **Express Your Goals**: Be clear about your ambitions, including your ISA certification pursuit and how you plan to achieve sales targets.
- **Showcase Your Research**: Demonstrate your understanding of SavATree&#x27;s services and how they compare to competitors.
- **Highlight Your Value**: Emphasize your unique blend of tech and green industry experience, positioning yourself as a valuable asset.

### Conclusion

Prepare thoroughly, be confident in your experience and skills, and express your passion for the role. Use the interview as an opportunity to showcase how you will contribute to SavATree’s success and growth. Good luck!

• Explain how your IT background enhances your ability to use technology in tree care
• Discuss how your military experience translates to project management in arboriculture
• Relate your sales experience to building client relationships in the green industry

My military experience taught me the importance of precision and safety in high-stakes environments, which directly applies to commercial tree care operations. As for sales, my time at ServiceNow honed my ability to understand client needs and propose tailored solutions. In the context of arboriculture, this means I can effectively assess a property&#x27;s needs, explain complex tree care concepts in accessible terms, and propose comprehensive care plans that align with the client&#x27;s goals and budget.&quot;

Showcase your technical knowledge of tree and plant health:
• Discuss specific tree diseases common in Texas and their treatment methods
• Explain your understanding of soil health and its impact on tree vitality
• Demonstrate knowledge of integrated pest management techniques

Sample answer: &quot;In Texas, we face challenges like oak wilt, hypoxylon canker, and bacterial leaf scorch. I&#x27;m well-versed in the latest treatment methods, including macro-infusion techniques for oak wilt and cultural practices to prevent hypoxylon canker. Moreover, my work with Soil Grower has deepened my understanding of soil health. I can explain to clients how factors like soil compaction, pH levels, and nutrient deficiencies affect tree health, and propose solutions like aeration, soil amendments, or custom fertilization programs. I&#x27;m also a proponent of integrated pest management. For instance, when dealing with cankerworms on pecan trees, I consider biological controls and targeted treatments before resorting to broad-spectrum insecticides.&quot;

Demonstrate your understanding of SavATree&#x27;s services and mission:
• Discuss SavATree&#x27;s comprehensive plant health care approach
• Mention specific SavATree services and how they benefit commercial properties
• Align your personal values with SavATree&#x27;s mission

Sample answer: &quot;SavATree&#x27;s comprehensive approach to plant health care aligns perfectly with my holistic view of landscape management. For commercial properties, services like your customized fertilization programs and professional pruning can significantly enhance property value and reduce long-term maintenance costs. This aligns with my personal mission to promote sustainable urban forestry.&quot;

• Discuss how your startup experience has honed your business acumen
• Explain how your knowledge of soil health technologies complements SavATree&#x27;s services
• Address potential conflicts of interest proactively

I&#x27;ve learned to identify market needs, develop innovative solutions, and effectively communicate the value of our services to clients.
