**ASSISTANT**:
SavATree offers a comprehensive range of proprietary products and services designed to enhance tree and plant health care. Here are some key proprietary products and services you should highlight in your interview:

1. **Tree and Shrub Fertilization**:
   - SavATree provides customized fertilization programs that include their proprietary nutrient blends designed to enhance the health and growth of trees and shrubs. These blends are tailored to address specific soil and plant needs, promoting robust growth and disease resistance.

2. **Organic Care Program**:
   - This program emphasizes the use of natural and organic products to care for trees, shrubs, and lawns. It includes organic fertilizers, biostimulants, and pest management solutions, ensuring environmentally friendly and sustainable care.

3. **Plant Health Care Programs**:
   - SavATree’s comprehensive plant health care programs include services such as insect and mite management, disease treatment, and soil health management. Their proprietary products in these programs help improve root system health and facilitate nutrient uptake, thereby enhancing overall plant vitality.

4. **Tick and Deer Protection**:
   - Proprietary products for tick control and deer repellent treatments, such as the &quot;Three Circles of Protection&quot; and &quot;Clear Repellent Treatments,&quot; are designed to protect properties from these pests while being safe for the environment.

5. **Winter Protection Treatments**:
   - SavATree offers specialized winter protection treatments to shield plants and trees from harsh winter conditions, ensuring their health and vitality through the colder months.

6. **Custom Blends for Lawns**:
   - SavATree’s lawn care services include proprietary fertilizer blends and treatment programs tailored to specific lawn needs, promoting lush, green lawns while managing weeds, diseases, and pests.

Understanding and emphasizing these proprietary products and services during your interview can showcase your knowledge of SavATree’s unique offerings and your alignment with their mission of sustainable and environmentally responsible tree and lawn care.

To excel in your upcoming interview with SavATree, it is essential to understand their product offerings, services, and company goals, particularly in the commercial sector. Here is a comprehensive summary to help you prepare:

### SavATree Overview
SavATree, established over 45 years ago, initially focused on combating the gypsy moth epidemic. The company has since expanded its services nationwide, offering tree, shrub, and lawn care with a commitment to environmental preservation and sustainability. SavATree prides itself on a holistic approach to plant health care, utilizing advanced techniques and proprietary products to maintain the health and beauty of landscapes【236†source】【237†source】.

### Proprietary Products
SavATree offers a range of proprietary products designed to enhance the health and vitality of trees, shrubs, and lawns. Some of these products include:

- **ArborKelp®**: A biostimulant that promotes root growth and stress resistance in trees.
- **Mycorrhizal Applications®**: Products that enhance nutrient uptake and soil health.
- **NutriRoot®**: A tree and shrub growth enhancer.
- **SavATree’s Custom Fertilization Programs**: Tailored to specific landscape needs, ensuring optimal plant health.
- **Insect and Disease Management Solutions**: Custom treatments to protect plants from pests and diseases.

### Commercial Services
SavATree&#x27;s commercial services are designed to cater to a variety of properties, including:
- **Apartments and HOA/Condo Complexes**
- **Office Parks**
- **Golf Courses and Country Clubs**
- **Hospitality Venues**
- **Municipal and Government Properties**
- **Public Gardens and Arboreta**
- **Schools and Colleges**

These services include tree pruning, removal, disease treatment, fertilization, and integrated pest management, all tailored to enhance the aesthetic and functional value of commercial landscapes【237†source】.
